[&#xA;                    http://blast.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/Blast.cgi?CMD=Web&amp;PAGE_TYPE=BlastHome&#xA;                    &#xA;                  ]" href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR116" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3088">116</a>] as the whole genomes are unavailable. Nucleotide-peptide matches were obtained with the Darwin [<a data-track="click" data-track-action="reference anchor" data-track-label="link" data-test="citation-ref" aria-label="Reference 107" title="Gonnet GH, Hallett MT, Korostensky C, Bernardin L: Darwin v. 2.0: an interpreted computer language for the biosciences. Bioinformatics. 2000, 16 (2): 101-103." href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR107" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3091">107</a>] bioinformatics platform.</p><h3 class="c-article__sub-heading" id="Sec40">Visualizazion</h3><p>The circular plot showing the correspondance betweeen the genetic and physical maps was created with Circos [<a data-track="click" data-track-action="reference anchor" data-track-label="link" data-test="citation-ref" aria-label="Reference 117" title="Krzywinski M, Schein J, Birol I, Connors J, Gascoyne R, Horsman D, Jones SJ, Marra MA: Circos: an information aesthetic for comparative genomics. Genome Res. 2009, 19 (9): 1639-1645." href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR117" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3102">117</a>]. The comparison of orthologous syntenic genomic regions of the SAL1 gene was created with CoGe [<a data-track="click" data-track-action="reference anchor" data-track-label="link" data-test="citation-ref" aria-label="Reference 43" title="Lyons E, Freeling M: How to usefully compare homologous plant genes and chromosomes as DNA sequences. Plant J. 2008, 53 (4): 661-673." href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR43" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3105">43</a>, <a data-track="click" data-track-action="reference anchor" data-track-label="link" data-test="citation-ref" aria-label="Reference 45" title="Lyons E, Pedersen B, Kane J, Alam M, Ming R, Tang H, Wang X, Bowers J, Paterson A, Lisch D, Freeling M: Finding and comparing syntenic regions among arabidopsis and the outgroups papaya, poplar, and grape: CoGe with rosids. Plant Physiol. 2008, 148 (4): 1772-1781." href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR45" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3108">45</a>] as was the dotplot of the syntenic map in Figure <a data-track="click" data-track-label="link" data-track-action="figure anchor" href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#Fig2">2</a>. Trees were visualized using FigTree v1.3.1 [<a data-track="click" data-track-action="reference anchor" data-track-label="link" data-test="citation-ref" aria-label="Reference 101" title="FigTree. [&#xA;                    http://tree.bio.ed.ac.uk/software/figtree/&#xA;                    &#xA;                  ]," href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR101" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3114">101</a>]. Gepard [<a data-track="click" data-track-action="reference anchor" data-track-label="link" data-test="citation-ref" aria-label="Reference 46" title="Krumsiek J, Arnold R, Rattei T: Gepard: a rapid and sensitive tool for creating dotplots on genome scale. Bioinformatics. 2007, 23 (8): 1026-1028." href="/articles/10.1186/1471-2164-15-581#ref-CR46" id="ref-link-section-d36917e3118">46</a>] was used to create the dotplot of the A and B genomes.</p><h3 class="c-article__sub-heading" id="Sec41">Availability of supporting data</h3><p>Data, analyses and updates can be downloaded from: <a href="http://www.tef-research.org/genome.html">http://www.tef-research.org/genome.html</a>.</p><p>The genome and maker annotations are available for viewing, blasting and download at CoGe at: <a href="https://genomevolution.org/CoGe/GenomeInfo.pl?gid=22790">https://genomevolution.org/CoGe/GenomeInfo.pl?gid=22790</a>.</p><p>The project is registered at NCBI with BioProject Number: <a href="http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/bioproject/253673">http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/bioproject/253673</a>.</p><p>The sample accessions are: SAMN02872936 (for GNY7); SAMN02872919 (GNY8); GNY9 and SAMN02872920 (GNY9).</p><p>Accession numbers in the Sequence Read Archive are: SRR1463375, SRR1463376, SRR1463377, SRR1463396, SRR1463397 and SRR1463402.</p></div></div></section>
